def olttj():
    def _tj():
        global users,self_olt
        for ah in users:
            if ah['trip'] in [ww['trip'] for ww in onlineuser]: ah['olt'] += 1
        self_olt += 1
        with open(r"/root/Python-3.10.6/files/self_olt.txt",'w') as oty:
            oty.write(str(self_olt))
        usd()
    while True:
        if onlineuser:
            threading.Thread(target=_tj).start()
        time.sleep(0.99)
